***шерсть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шерсть.html>шерсть</a> (3864)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сьрсть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sĭrstĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, (since the 14th century) <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">шьрсть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šĭrstĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sьrstь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱer(s)-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rough hair, bristle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-tь</i>, whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">šerys</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hair</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шерсть.html>шерсть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šerstʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шерсть.html>ше́рсти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шерсть.html>ше́рсти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шерсть.html>шерсте́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fur, hair (animal hair or human body hair; contrast <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:мех.html>мех</a>)</li>
<li>wool (hair of an animal used to make clothing)</li>
<li>woollen cloth, worsted, wadding</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шерсть.html>шерсть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šerstʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-яно́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-janój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шерстяной.html>шерстяно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šerstjanój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wool; woolen, woollen</li>
<li>wooly</li></ol>

***шершавый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шершавый.html>шершавый</a> (8484)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шершавый.html>шерша́в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šeršáv</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rough</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which per Vasmer comes either from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">шьрсть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šĭrstĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> -and is thus cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шерсть.html>шерсть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šerstʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>- or from a root related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шорох.html>шо́рох</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šórox</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rustle, murmur</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">шереха́тий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šerexátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">ше́рхаць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šérhacʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">sŕšati</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шершавый.html>шерша́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šeršávyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)шерша́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)шерша́вей</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шест.html>шест</a> (9750)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šьstъ</i>

***шествие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шествие.html>ше́ствие</a> (10957)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">шьствие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šĭstvie</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Constructed from the root of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šьdlъ</i> (resultative participle, later past tense, of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьstvo</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьje</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">idtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шествие.html>ше́ствие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šéstvije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шествие.html>ше́ствия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шествие.html>ше́ствия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шествие.html>ше́ствий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>procession, demonstration</li></ol>

***шествовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шествовать.html>ше́ствовать</a> (15067)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ше́ств(ие)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šéstv(ije)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шествовать.html>ше́ствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šéstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прошествовать.html>проше́ствовать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to walk (slowly with procession)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шестеренка.html>шестерёнка</a> (26208)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шестеренка.html>шестерёнка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šesterjónka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шестеренка.html>шестерёнка</a></b>

***шестерка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шестерка.html>шестёрка</a> (8218)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шестерка.html>шестёрка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šestjórka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шестерка.html>шестёрки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шестерка.html>шестёрки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шестерка.html>шестёрок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> six</li>
<li>group of six</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> six
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырной.html>козырна́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шестерка.html>шестёрка</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kozyrnaja <b>šestjórka</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">six of trumps</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>No 6 bus tram, etc</li>
<li>six-in-hand</li>
<li>six-oar boat</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> underling, minion</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства_2"></span></h3>
<p><b>шес<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тёр</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-шест-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ёр-к</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шестеро.html>ше́стеро</a> (7498)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шестеро.html>ше́стеро</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šéstero</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>six (in a group together), six of them
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шестеро.html>ше́стеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šéstero</b> detéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">six children</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шестеро.html>ше́стеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šéstero</b> časóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">six watches</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шестеро.html>ше́стеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šéstero</b> očkóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">six pairs of glasses</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шестеро.html>ше́стеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šéstero</b> iz nas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">six of us</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шестеро.html>ше́стеро</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nas býlo <b>šéstero</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there were six of us</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The nominative of a collective numeral governs the genitive plural of the noun, pronoun, or adjective. The other cases agree with that of the noun, pronoun, or adjective. Not used with feminine nouns. Used mostly when speaking of children and with a few nouns that are used in the plural only, such as <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очки́</a>, or with pronouns.
</p>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p>Числительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:собирательный.html>собира́тельное</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-шест-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ер</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-о</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***шестнадцать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шестнадцать.html>шестна́дцать</a> (4250)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compounded from <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шесть.html>шесть</a></b> + <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> + <b>дцать</b>, or <i>six on ten</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шестнадцать.html>шестна́дцать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šestnádcatʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sixteen (16)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:шестнадцать.html>шестна́дцать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šestnadcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шестнадцать.html>шестна́дцать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šestnádcatʹ</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sixteen boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шестнадцать.html>шестна́дцатью</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>šestnádcatʹju</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with sixteen boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шестнадцать.html>шестна́дцать</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>šestnádcatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately sixteen boys</span></div></li></ul>

***шесть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шесть.html>шесть</a> (742)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šestь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*swéḱs</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_2">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шесть.html>шесть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šestʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>six (6)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:шесть.html>шесть</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шесть.html>шесть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šestʹ</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">six boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шесть.html>шестью́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>šestʹjú</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with six boys</span></div></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шестьдесят.html>шестьдеся́т</a> (2864)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compounded from <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шесть.html>шесть</a></b> + <b><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a></b>, or <i>six tens</i>. <b>Десят</b> was the <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span></span> genitive plural, which is required by numbers <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> and up.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шестьдесят.html>шестьдеся́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šestʹdesját</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sixty (60)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>

<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́х</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шестьсот.html>шестиста́х</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:солдат.html>солда́тах</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní govoríli o svoíx <b>šestistáx</b> soldátax.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They were talking about their <b>six hundred</b> soldiers.</span></div></li></ul>

***шибко.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шибко.html>ши́бко</a> (6135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ши́бкий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šíbkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шибко.html>ши́бко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šíbko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fast, quickly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hard, much
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шибко.html>ши́бко</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударить.html>уда́рить</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šíbko</b> udáritʹ kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give smb a hard knock</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шибко.html>ши́бко</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скучать.html>скуча́ет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>šíbko</b> skučájet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is very lonely</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***шивший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>ши́вший</a> (7123)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>ши́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šívšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***шикарный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шикарный.html>шика́рный</a> (6994)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шикарный.html>шика́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šikárnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>chic, smart, splendid, grand, magnificent, stylish (elegant)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b>ши<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кара.html>ка́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-шикарн-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***шило.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>ши́ло</a> (11414)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šidlo</i>, composed of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ši</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-dlo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(tool suffix)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">šídlo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">awl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sūbula</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">awl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>ши́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šílo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>ши́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шило.html>ши́лья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шило.html>ши́льев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>awl
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>ши́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мешок.html>мешке́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утаить.html>утаи́шь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">šíla v mešké ne utaíšʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">murder will out</span></div></dd>

</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">chenille</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шинель.html>шине́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šinélʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шинель.html>шине́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шинель.html>шине́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шинель.html>шине́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> uniform overcoat</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šipъ</i>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шип.html>шип</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šip</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шип.html>шипа́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шип.html>шипы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шип.html>шипо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thorn, spine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:роза.html>ро́зы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шип.html>шипо́в</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne byvájet rózy bez <b>šipóv</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Every rose has its <b>thorn</b></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">There doesn't exist a rose without thorns</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>stud <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">small object that protrudes from something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шина.html>ши́ны</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шип.html>шипа́ми</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">šíny s <b>šipámi</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>studded</b> tires/tyres</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>cleat <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">protrusion on the sole of a shoe</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">construction</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tenon, pin</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> journal <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">part of a shaft or axle that rests on bearings</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
